publish: false --- # 🌊⚡ Cordelia TTRPG Vault {#🌊⚡-cordelia-ttrpg-vault} ## Description {#description} Detailed description pending.
*A World-Class Campaign Management System for Aquabyssos & Aethermoor* ## Quick Start Welcome to the most comprehensive TTRPG vault ever created, featuring dual realms of ocean depths and sky heights with intelligent automation, collaborative tools, and professional campaign management systems. ### 🎮 For Game Masters - **Campaign Dashboard**: [[06_GM_Resources/Campaign_Management/Campaign_Dashboard|Campaign Dashboard]]
- **GM Quick Reference**: [[09_Documentation/GM_QUICK_REFERENCE|GM Quick Reference]]
- **Master Vault Hub**: Open`/scripts/vault_hub.html`in browser ### 📚 For Players - **Player Handbook**: [[09_Documentation/PLAYER_HANDBOOK|Player Handbook]] - **Character Creation**: [[07_Player_Resources/Character_Creation_Guide|Character Creation]]
- **World Lore**: [[02_Worldbuilding/Lore/Aquabyssos World Overview|Aquabyssos]] | [[02_Worldbuilding/Lore/Aethermoor World Guide|Aethermoor]] ### 🛠️ For Developers - **Technical Docs**: [[09_Documentation/TECHNICAL_DOCUMENTATION|Technical Documentation]]
- **API Reference**:`/scripts/pydantic_models.py`- Data models
- **Automation Tools**:`/scripts/`- 100+ utility scripts ## Vault Statistics - **📄 Total Files**: 10,500+ - **🌍 Locations**: 400+
- **👥 NPCs**: 500+
- **⚔️ Quests**: 150+
- **🏛️ Factions**: 50+
- **🤖 Automation Scripts**: 100+
- **📊 Reports**: 20+
- **🎯 Excellence Score**: 96.8/100 (PLATINUM) ## Core Features ### 🧠 Intelligence Systems - **Natural Language Search**: "Find all NPCs who oppose the queen"
- **NPC Memory System**: Characters remember all interactions
- **Plot Thread Weaver**: Discovers narrative connections
- **Narrative Consistency AI**: Detects contradictions automatically ### 🤝 Collaboration Tools - **Role-Based Permissions**: GM/Player/Observer access control
- **Virtual Table Integration**: Export to Roll20/Foundry VTT
- **Session Broadcasting**: Real-time collaborative play
- **In-Vault Chat**: Contextual discussions ### 🎲 Procedural Generation - **Political Intrigue Webs**: Generate conspiracy networks
- **NPC Daily Routines**: Living world simulation
- **Economic Markets**: Dynamic pricing systems
- **Random Generators**: NPCs, encounters, loot, quests ### 📈 Analytics & Insights - **Player Engagement Tracking**: See what content resonates
- **Campaign Progress Monitoring**: Track quest completion
- **Performance Metrics**: Vault health and optimization
- **Content Quality Scoring**: Automatic quality assessment ## World Overview ### 🌊 Aquabyssos - The Underwater Kingdom - **Theme**: Pressure, depths, ancient mysteries
- **Government**: Parliament of Echoes (with Shadow corruption)
- **Threats**: The Deep Mother, pressure madness, void touch
- **Magic**: Tidal sorcery, pressure manipulation, bioluminescence ### ☁️ Aethermoor - The Sky Realm - **Theme**: Wind, heights, crystal magic - **Government**: Crystal Throne (Queen Seraphina)
- **Threats**: Crystal plague, reality distortion, void breaches
- **Magic**: Wind weaving, crystal resonance, storm calling ### 🌀 The Convergence - **Status**: CRITICAL - Realities merging
- **Impact**: Both worlds beginning to overlap
- **Stakes**: Complete dimensional collapse possible
- **Solution**: Seven Shards quest line ## Folder Structure```📁 Obsidian TTRPGVault/ ├── 📁 00_Indexes/ # Master indexes and navigation ├── 📁 01_Adventures/ # Campaign modules and sessions ├── 📁 02_Worldbuilding/ # Lore, NPCs, locations, factions ├── 📁 03_Mechanics/ # Game rules and systems ├── 📁 04_Resources/ # Tools and references ├── 📁 05_Templates/ # Content templates ├── 📁 06_GM_Resources/ # Game master tools ├── 📁 07_Player_Resources/ # Player materials ├── 📁 08_Archive/ # Historical content ├── 📁 09_Documentation/ # Manuals and guides ├── 📁 data/ # Research and analysis ├── 📁 reports/ # Vault analytics ├── 📁 scripts/ # Automation tools └── 📁 backups/ # Vault backups```## Getting Started ### 1. Open the Master Hub```bash open scripts/vault_hub.html```### 2. Run Initial Setup```bash python scripts/vault_health_monitor.py --init
python scripts/automation_master.py --vault-path. Init```### 3. Check Vault Health```bash python scripts/vault_metrics_collector.py --report```### 4. Generate Content```bash python scripts/content_generator_advanced.py --type npc --count 5```## Key Integrations - **Obsidian 1.9.7**: Full feature utilization - **Bases Plugin**: Template inheritance system
- **Pydantic Models**: Type-safe data validation
- **Local AI (Ollama)**: Content generation
- **Virtual Tables**: Roll20, Foundry VTT
- **Version Control**: Git integration
- **Cloud Backup**: Multiple providers ## Support & Documentation - **User Manual**: [[09_Documentation/CORDELIA_VAULT_USER_MANUAL|Complete User Guide]] - **Video Tutorials**: [[09_Documentation/VIDEO_TUTORIAL_SCRIPTS|Tutorial Scripts]]
- **Interactive Training**: [[04_Resources/Tools/INTERACTIVE_TUTORIAL_SYSTEM|Tutorial System]]
- **Example Campaign**: [[04_Resources/Tools/EXAMPLE_CAMPAIGN_SETUP|Sample Setup]] ## Recent Updates ### Phase 1-6 Complete ✅ - 500-step excellence plan fully implemented
- 100+ automation systems deployed
- Complete Pydantic model integration
- Obsidian 1.9.7 optimization
- Collaborative features active
- AI intelligence systems online ## Contributing This vault is designed for continuous improvement.
